#14th Business Cycle
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.900101
	title = mdmosjap_japan.900101.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.900101.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
		NOT = {
			has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_bubble_burst
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KENKIHO_RECESSION
		}
		num_of_civilian_factories > 64
		#date < 2005.12.31
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.900101.oA
		set_country_flag = disable_cycle_costs
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = stable_growth }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stable_growth add_idea = fast_growth }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = stagnation }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stagnation add_idea = stable_growth }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = recession }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = recession add_idea = stagnation }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = depression }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = depression add_idea = recession }
		}
		clr_country_flag = disable_cycle_costs
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = stable_growth
					has_idea = fast_growth
					has_idea = economic_boom
				}
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		#swap_ideas = { remove_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_large_boned add_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_14th_cycle }		#OBSOLETED
	}
}

#Unrest 0: Politically Controversial TV Program (Left Unrest)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.100101
	title = mdmosjap_japan.100101.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.100101.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 9600
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_0 = yes
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_1 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_10 = yes
			factor = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_25 = yes
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_50 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAP_NF_MEDIA_TOT2 }
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			JAP = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_SENTENCED
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_INVOKED
				}
			}
			factor = 32
		}
	}
	
	#Defend Protester
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.100101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.100101.oA"
		add_political_power = -10
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_2 = yes
	}
	
	#Neutral
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.100101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.100101.oB"
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
	}
	
	#Attack Protester
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.100101.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.100101.oC"
		add_political_power = -10
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_2 = yes
	}
}

	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

		original_tag = JAP
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 28800
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_0 = yes
			factor = 100
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_1 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_10 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_25 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_50 = yes
			factor = 0.05
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_75 = yes
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NATIONAL_WORRYING
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			JAP = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_SENTENCED
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_INVOKED
				}
			}
			factor = 32
		}
	}
	
	#We don't need any sensitive supports like these radicalist.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.102101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.102101.oA"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_2 = yes
		add_political_power = -100
	}
	
	#Thanks, I Hate it.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0.01
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.102101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.102101.oB"
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
	}
	
	#They would be cultivated as a good supporters.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0.01
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.102101.oC

#Unrest 75: Government's Blame against Mass Media (Leftist Government)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.103101
	title = mdmosjap_japan.103101.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.103101.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
		OR = {
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_INVOKED }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 21600
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_0 = yes
			factor = 1000
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_1 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_10 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_25 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_50 = yes
			factor = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_75 = yes
			factor = 0.01
		}
		modifier = {
			trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_left_90 = yes
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NATIONAL_WORRYING
			factor = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			has_stability < 0.50
			factor = 20
		}
		modifier = {
			JAP = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_SENTENCED
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_INVOKED
				}
			}
			factor = 32
		}
	}
	
	#Government is right
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.103101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.103101.oA"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		add_stability = -0.01
	}
	
	#We must close our mouths now
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } }

					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } }
				}
				factor = 4
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.110301.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.110301.oB"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_1_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_6_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_7_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_20_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_21_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_22_var_2 = yes
	}
}

#Japan Declared War against North Korea!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.200201
	title = mdmosjap_japan.200201.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.200201.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = KOR
		JAP = {
			has_war_with = NKO
			OR = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
			}
		}
		NKO = { has_capitulated = no }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR
	}
	
	#We will fight togerther! For the Unification!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.200201.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.200201.oA"
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member }
			remove_ideas = sco_member
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_observer }
			remove_ideas = sco_observer
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member_econ }
			remove_ideas = sco_member_econ
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member_pol }
			remove_ideas = sco_member_pol
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member_mil }
			remove_ideas = sco_member_mil
		}
		add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "NKO" value = 1000 }
		NKO = { add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = ROOT value = 1000 } }
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
	#	create_wargoal = { target = NKO type = take_core_state }
		declare_war_on = { target = NKO type = take_core_state }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
				JAP = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
				add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "NKO" value = 1000 }
			}
			add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "NKO" value = 1000 }
		} else = {
			create_faction = mdmosjap_faction_JAP_apda_alliance
			create_wargoal = { target = NKO type = take_core_state }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
				}
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
				add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "NKO" value = 1000 }
			}
			add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "NKO" value = 1000 }
		} else = {
			create_faction = mdmosjap_faction_JAP_apda_alliance
			create_wargoal = { target = NKO type = take_core_state }
		}
	}
	
	#We will fight, but we need a preparation at this now.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.200201.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.200201.oB"
		add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "NKO" value = 1000 }
		create_wargoal = { target = NKO type = take_core_state }
		add_ai_strategy = { type = declare_war id = "NKO" value = 200 }
	}
}

#Japan Declared War against South Korea!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.200203
	title = mdmosjap_japan.200203.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.200203.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = NKO
		JAP = {
			has_war_with = KOR
			OR = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
			}
		}
		KOR = { has_capitulated = no }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR
	}
	
	#We will fight togerther! For the Unification!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.200203.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.200203.oA"
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member }
			remove_ideas = sco_member
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_observer }
			remove_ideas = sco_observer
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member_econ }
			remove_ideas = sco_member_econ
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member_pol }
			remove_ideas = sco_member_pol
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member_mil }
			remove_ideas = sco_member_mil
		}
		add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "KOR" value = 1000 }
		KOR = { add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = ROOT value = 1000 } }
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
	#	create_wargoal = { target = KOR type = take_core_state }
		declare_war_on = { target = KOR type = take_core_state }

			limit = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member

					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
				add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "KOR" value = 1000 }
			}
			add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "KOR" value = 1000 }
			
		} else = {
			create_faction = mdmosjap_faction_JAP_apda_alliance
			create_wargoal = { target = KOR type = take_core_state }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
				}
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member

#Foreign Occupation Zone in the Korean Peninsula
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.200301
	title = mdmosjap_japan.200301.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.200301.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR
		NOT = { has_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_CONFERENCE_EXECUTED }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				ROOT = {
					tag = KOR
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_LOSER }
					has_war = no
				}
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							tag = NKO
							has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_LOSER
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { tag = ROOT }
							NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
							NKO = {
								AND = {
									has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_LOSER
									exists = yes
									OR = {
										is_puppet_of = PREV
										is_subject_of = PREV
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				ROOT = {
					tag = NKO
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_LOSER }
					has_war = no
				}
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							tag = KOR
							has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_LOSER
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { tag = ROOT }
							NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
							KOR = {
								AND = {
									has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_LOSER
									exists = yes
									OR = {
										is_puppet_of = PREV
										is_subject_of = PREV
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				ROOT = {
					OR = {
						tag = KOR
						tag = NKO
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_LOSER }
					has_war = no
				}
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
						OR = {
							controls_state = 601
							controls_state = 602
							controls_state = 603
							controls_state = 604
							controls_state = 605
							controls_state = 606
							controls_state = 607
							controls_state = 608
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_CONFERENCE_EXECUTED
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }
	
	#Demand to Return Our Soil Immediately
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.200301.oA

#Fall of South Korea / North Korea Transition Government
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.200308
	title = mdmosjap_japan.200308.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.200308.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.200308.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.200308.oA"
		#GAME OVER
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { state = 601 }
				NOT = { state = 602 }
				NOT = { state = 603 }
				NOT = { state = 604 }
				NOT = { state = 605 }
				NOT = { state = 606 }
				NOT = { state = 607 }
				NOT = { state = 608 }
			}
			ROOT = { overlord = { transfer_state = PREV.PREV } }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = ROOT
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_KOR_TRANSITION } }
			KOR = { annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = NO } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_NKO_TRANSITION } }
			NKO = { annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = NO } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_KOJ_TRANSITION } }
			KOJ = { annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = NO } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_KOREAN_RECOLONISATION_IN_PROGRESS } } }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = {
					overlord = {
						transfer_state = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.410101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.410101.oB"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ANTICCP_IS_IN_THE_WAR_WITH_CHINA
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
				}
				NOT = { has_war_with = CHI }
			}
			country_event = mdmosjap_japan.410103
		}
	}
	
	#Call the APDA Allies!
	option = {
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.410101.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.410101.oC"

		}

#Anti-CCP Member Needs Our Help!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.410103
	title = mdmosjap_japan.410103.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.410103.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Declare the War against China Now!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				is_ai = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.410103.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.410103.oA"
		add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "CHI" value = 1000 }
		CHI = { add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = ROOT value = 1000 } }
		add_political_power = 100
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { CHI = { any_controlled_state = { is_core_of = ROOT } } }
			create_wargoal = { target = CHI type = take_core_state }
			declare_war_on = { target = CHI type = take_core_state }
	#	} else = {
	#		create_wargoal = { target = CHI type = topple_government }
	#		declare_war_on = { target = CHI type = topple_government }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
				}
				any_other_country = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
				add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "CHI" value = 1000 }
			}
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = FROM enemy = CHI }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "CHI" value = 1000 }
		} else = {
			create_faction = mdmosjap_faction_JAP_anticcp_alliance
			declare_war_on = { target = CHI type = annex_everything }
		}
	}
	
	#We will fight, but we need a preparation at this now.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.410103.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.410103.oB"
		add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "CHI" value = 1000 }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ANTICCP_IS_IN_THE_WAR_WITH_CHINA_DECISION_PREPARATION
		add_political_power = 100
	}
}

#Japan Declared War against China!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.410201
	title = mdmosjap_japan.410201.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.410201.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TAI
		JAP = { has_war_with = CHI }
		CHI = { has_capitulated = no }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }
	
	#We will fight togerther! For the Unification!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.410201.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.410201.oA"
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member }
			remove_ideas = sco_member
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_observer }
			remove_ideas = sco_observer
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member_econ }
			remove_ideas = sco_member_econ
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member_pol }
			remove_ideas = sco_member_pol
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = sco_member_mil }
			remove_ideas = sco_member_mil
		}
		add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "CHI" value = 1000 }
		CHI = { add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = ROOT value = 1000 } }
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { CHI = { any_controlled_state = { is_core_of = ROOT } } }
			create_wargoal = { target = CHI type = take_core_state }
			declare_war_on = { target = CHI type = take_core_state }
		} else = {
			create_wargoal = { target = CHI type = topple_government }
			declare_war_on = { target = CHI type = topple_government }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
				any_other_country = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
				add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "CHI" value = 1000 }
			}
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = FROM enemy = CHI }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "CHI" value = 1000 }
		} else = {
			create_faction = mdmosjap_faction_JAP_apda_alliance
			declare_war_on = { target = CHI type = annex_everything }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
				}
				any_other_country = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Leader_of_NATO }
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
				add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "CHI" value = 1000 }
			}
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = FROM enemy = CHI }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "CHI" value = 1000 }
		} else = {
			create_faction = mdmosjap_faction_JAP_anticcp_alliance
			declare_war_on = { target = CHI type = annex_everything }
		}
	}
	
	#We will fight, but we need a preparation at this now.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.410201.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.410201.oB"
		add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "CHI" value = 1000 }
		create_wargoal = { target = CHI type = take_core_state }
	}
}

#The New York Conference
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.490100
	title = mdmosjap_japan.490100.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.490100.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
	#	tag = JAP
		has_game_rule = {
			rule = mdmosjap_gamerules_option_atami_conference
			option = MDMOSJAP_GAMERULES_OPTION_ATAMI_CONFERENCE_ON
		}
		ROOT = { 
			NOT = { tag = TAI }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
						has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
					}
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees }
					NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1 }
					NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2 }
					NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member }
					NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member }
					is_faction_leader = yes
					any_allied_country = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
						}
						NOT = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			is_in_faction_with = TAI
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
		#	country_exists = TAI
			has_war_with = CHI
		}
		TAI = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
			}
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
		#	is_faction_leader = no
			has_war_with = CHI
		}
		CHI = {
			OR = {
				is_subject = no
				is_puppet = no
			}
			has_war_with = TAI
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = TAI }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						#In Case of Manchuria Strat
						AND = {
							NOT = { controls_state = 548 }		#Tianjin
							NOT = { controls_state = 552 }		#Dalian
						}
						
						#In Case of Chinese Sea Strat
						AND = {
							NOT = { controls_state = 435 }		#Qingdao
							NOT = { controls_state = 540 }		#Shanghai
							NOT = { controls_state = 536 }		#Nanjing
							NOT = { controls_state = 538 }		#Hangzhou
							NOT = { controls_state = 510 }		#Xiamen
							NOT = { controls_state = 532 }		#Pearl River Delta
							AND = {
								NOT = { country_exists = HKG }
								NOT = { controls_state = 595 }		#Hong Kong
							}
							HKG = {
								is_subject_of = CHI
								is_puppet_of = CHI
								has_capitulated = yes
							}
						}
						
						#In Case of Land Strat
						AND = {
							NOT = { controls_state = 558 }		#Taiyuan
							NOT = { controls_state = 567 }		#Luoyang
							NOT = { controls_state = 564 }		#Anqing
							NOT = { controls_state = 562 }		#Nanchang
							NOT = { controls_state = 572 }		#Changsha
							
							NOT = { controls_state = 570 }		#Wuhan
							NOT = { controls_state = 583 }		#Chongqing
							NOT = { controls_state = 578 }		#Kunming
							NOT = { controls_state = 586 }		#Chengdu
							
							NOT = { controls_state = 560 }		#Lanzhou
							NOT = { controls_state = 559 }		#Xi'an
						}
					}
				}
				surrender_progress > 0.75
			} else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { controls_state = 547 }		#Beijing
				}
				surrender_progress > 0.75
			} else = {
				surrender_progress > 0.80
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_HAD_ATAMI_CONFERENCE_BUT_REFUSED
	}
	
	#Demand the unconditional surrender
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.490100.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.490100.oA"
		CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.490101 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#No one wants any disadvantageous bitter peace like this
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.490100.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.490100.oB"
		TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.490102 days = 1 } }

#Dissolve of Anti-CCP Network?
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.499101
	title = mdmosjap_japan.499101.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.499101.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_war = no
		has_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_THIRD_SINO_JAPANESE_WAR
		OR = {
			has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
			has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
			has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
		#	has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
		}
	#	is_faction_leader = yes
		any_other_country = {
			is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			has_war = no
		}
		CHI = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
				exists = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
						}
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
							has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
						}
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					AND = {
						any_allied_country = {
							OR = {
								has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
								has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
								has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
								has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
							}
							is_in_faction_with = THIS
						}
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	
	#Every member has the option
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.499101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.499101.oA"
		
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ANTICCP_MEMBER_LEADER_LEAVABLE
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		#	country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.499103 days = 1 random = 24 random_days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.499103 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	#Dissolve the coalition
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.499101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.499101.oB"
		
		if = { limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees } remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1 } remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1 }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2 } remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2 }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member } remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member }
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_ANTICCP_MEMBER } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_ANTICCP_MEMBER }
		}
		
		ROOT = {
			calc_mdmosjap_anticcp_member = yes
			set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count = 0 }
			recalc_mdmosjap_anticcp_member = yes
			update_mdmosjap_anticcp_for_members = yes
		}
		
		add_named_threat = { threat = -20.0 name = MDMOSJAP_anticcp_network_dismantled }
		
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
				}
			}
			country_event = mdmosjap_japan.499102
		}
		
		news_event = { id = mdmosjap_japannews.499102 days = 1 }
	}
}

#Leaving from Anti-CCP Network?
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.499103
	title = mdmosjap_japan.499103.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.499103.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Leave now, immediately.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = { 
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.499103.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.499103.oA"
		
		leave_faction = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
			add_named_threat = { threat = -2.0 name = MDMOSJAP_anticcp_network_left }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1 }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
			add_named_threat = { threat = -2.0 name = MDMOSJAP_anticcp_network_left }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2 }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
			add_named_threat = { threat = -2.0 name = MDMOSJAP_anticcp_network_left }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
			add_named_threat = { threat = -2.0 name = MDMOSJAP_anticcp_network_left }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_ANTICCP_MEMBER } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_ANTICCP_MEMBER }
		}
		
		remove_from_array = { global.mdmosjap_anticcp_member = ROOT }
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count
			}
			calc_mdmosjap_anticcp_member = yes
			subtract_from_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count = 1 }
			recalc_mdmosjap_anticcp_member = yes
			update_mdmosjap_anticcp_for_members = yes
		}
		
		FROM = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.499104 }
	}
	
	#Not at this time.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				has_government = neutrality
				factor = 0.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_idea = ASEAN_member
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						tag = TAI
						tag = RAJ
						any_controlled_state = { is_neighbor_of = CHI }
					}
					CHI = {
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
						NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					tag = TAI
					any_other_country = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_HAD_ATAMI_CONFERENCE_BUT_REFUSED }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						tag = KOR
						NKO = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_LOSER }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = NKO
						KOR = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SECOND_KOREAN_WAR_LOSER }
					}
				}
				factor = 0.02
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees }
					NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1 }
					NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2 }
					has_idea = NATO_member
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.499103.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.499103.oB"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ANTICCP_LEAVABLE
	}
}

	option = {

			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				has_government = fascism

			}

		}

				}

				}

		}

		}

			add_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
		}
		
		add_to_array = { global.mdmosjap_apda_member = ROOT }
		
		ROOT = {
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_APDA_MEMBER
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_APDA_MEMBER } } }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_APDA_MEMBER }
			}
		}
		
		FROM = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.3000202 }
	#	CHI = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.3000204 }
		
		set_rule = { can_not_declare_war = yes }
		
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { MDACCESS_ACT_mdmosjap_clearvalue_FROM_influence_with_CHI = yes } }
	}
	
	#Disagree
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					any_controlled_state = {
						is_claimed_by = CHI
						is_owned_by = CHI
					}
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					any_controlled_state = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = ROOT
							is_core_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = sunni
							has_idea = shia
							has_idea = ibadi
							has_idea = sufi_islam
							has_government = fascism
						}
					}
					CHI = {
						controls_state = 592	#Xinjiang
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
				}
				factor = 0.2
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					CHI = {
						NOT = { has_idea = NATO_member }
						NOT = { has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally }
					}
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_government = communism }
					OR = {
						tag = TAI
						tag = RAJ
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_idea = Sino_Indian_Tensions
				factor = 0
			}
		}

				recalc_mdmosjap_apda_member = yes
				update_mdmosjap_apda_for_members = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.3000202.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.3000202.oA"
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_apda_member }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_apda_member }
		ROOT = {
			give_guarantee = FROM
			diplomatic_relation = { country = FROM relation = guarantee active = yes }
		}
		FROM = {
			give_guarantee = ROOT
			diplomatic_relation = { country = ROOT relation = guarantee active = yes }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member }
			give_guarantee = FROM
			diplomatic_relation = { country = FROM relation = guarantee active = yes }
		}
		country_event = mdmosjap_japan.3000203
	}
}

		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_refugeepop_MEN_MAX = 100 }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_refugeepop_MAN_MAX = 100 }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_refugeepop_TAI_MAX = 100 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.3000301.oA

		add_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees

					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_ANTICCP_MEMBER }
				}
				calc_mdmosjap_anticcp_member = yes
				recalc_mdmosjap_anticcp_member = yes
			}
		}
	}

					has_idea = sco_member
					has_idea = sco_member_econ
					has_idea = sco_member_pol
					has_idea = sco_member_mil
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = communism
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.3000601.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.3000601.oA"
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member } }
			add_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
		}
		
		add_to_array = { global.mdmosjap_anticcp_member = ROOT }
		
		ROOT = {
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ANTICCP_MEMBER
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_ANTICCP_MEMBER } } }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_ANTICCP_MEMBER }
			}
		}
		
		FROM = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.3000602 }
		CHI = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.3000604 }
		
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { MDACCESS_ACT_mdmosjap_clearvalue_FROM_influence_with_CHI = yes } }
	}
	
	#Disagree
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					any_controlled_state = {
						is_claimed_by = CHI
						is_owned_by = CHI
					}
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					any_controlled_state = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = ROOT
							is_core_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = sunni
							has_idea = shia
							has_idea = ibadi
							has_idea = sufi_islam
							has_government = fascism
						}
					}
					CHI = {
						controls_state = 592	#Xinjiang
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
				}
				factor = 0.2
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					CHI = {
						NOT = { has_idea = NATO_member }
						NOT = { has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally }
					}
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_government = communism }
					OR = {
						tag = TAI
						tag = RAJ
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_idea = Sino_Indian_Tensions
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.3000601.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.3000601.oB"
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.3000605 days = 1 } }
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { MDACCESS_ACT_mdmosjap_clearvalue_FROM_influence_with_CHI = yes } }
	}

#Ex-Sekigun Terrorist Fusako Shigenobu Released From the 20 Years Term
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.121107101
	title = mdmosjap_japan.121107101.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.121107101.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SHIGENOBU_ARRESTED
	}
	
	#Release Shigenobu
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = JAP_article_of_state_emergency_prerogative
					OR = {
						trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_rightwing_government = yes
						trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_islamist_government = yes
						has_country_leader = { name = "Shinzo Abe" }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.121107101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.121107101.oA executed"
		add_stability = -0.01
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_4_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_5_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_19_var_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		ISR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = recent_actions_negative } }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SHIGENOBU_RELEASED_LEGALLY
	}
	
	#Arrest Shigenobu Again
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = JAP_article_of_state_emergency_prerogative
			OR = {
				trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_rightwing_government = yes
				trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_islamist_government = yes
				has_country_leader = { name = "Shinzo Abe" }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_centrist_government = yes
					trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_leftwing_government = yes
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_article_of_state_emergency_prerogative }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.121107101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.121107101.oB executed"
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_5 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_5 = yes
		decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		ISR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = recent_actions_positive } }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SHIGENOBU_ARRESTED_AGAIN_ILLEGALLY
	}
}

country_event = {

			modifier = {

			}	
		}

			OR = {

				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
			}
		}

		add_political_power = -100
	}

			factor = 50
		}

			AND = {
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 } }
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } }
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } }
			}
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130129001.oB"

					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.130129001.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130129001.oC"
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.01 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.01 }
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.130129002 days = 1443 } }	#Scandal of Political Pressure against NHK (2005/1/12)
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Junichiro Koizumi" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Taku Yamasaki" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Shinzo Abe" }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.130129002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130129002.oA"
	#	add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = -0.05 }
	#	add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = -0.05 }

		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_21_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_22_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_23_var_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_2 = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Koichi Kato" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 100
		} else = {
			add_political_power = -400
		}
	}

	option = {

			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Koichi Kato" }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.130129002.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130129002.oB"
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Junichiro Koizumi" } }
			add_political_power = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Koichi Kato" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
			}
			add_stability = -0.10
			add_political_power = -500
		} else = {

		}

	#	add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.03 }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Passed
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}	
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.131102001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.131102001.oA"
		add_war_support = 0.01
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAP_ANTI_TERRORISM_LAW
	}
	
	#Rejected
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}	
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.131102001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.131102001.oB"
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_3 = yes
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japannews.131222001
	title = mdmosjap_japannews.131222001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japannews.131222001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	major = yes
	
	#Japan
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.131222001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.131222001.oA"
	}
	
	#North Korea
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = NKO
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.131222001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.131222001.oB"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
				NOT = { tag = NKO }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.131222001.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.131222001.oC"
	}
}

#Battle of Amamioshima: Japan's Action
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.131222002
	title = mdmosjap_japan.131222002.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.131222002.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		JAP = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_BATTLE_OF_AMAMIOSHIMA }
	}
	
	#Ask China
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		name = mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oA"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		CHI = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.131222003 }
	}
	
	#Keep Calm
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oB"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_4 = yes
		#add_national_unity = -0.05
		#add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.05 }
		mdmosjap_decrease_ruling_party_popularity_5 = yes
		NKO = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		}
	}
	
	#Violate EEZ
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				has_government = nationalist
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.131222002.oC"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_4 = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.05 }
		add_named_threat = { threat = 0.2 name = MDMOSJAP_JAP_PRCeez_violation_after_amamioshima }
		CHI = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.131222006 }
		TAI = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.131222007 }
	}
}

}

#Koichi Kato Left the Diet (Mutually With mdmosjap_japan_kato.101)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.140402001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.140402001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.140402001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
		date > 2002.3.0
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_FAILED_SUCCESSFULLY
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Koichi Kato" } }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_EXECUTED }
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_KATO_ONCE_QUIT_FROM_DIET }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_KATO_ONCE_QUIT_FROM_DIET
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.140402001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.140402001.oA"
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_1_var_1 = yes
		set_country_flag = { flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_KOICHI_KATO days = 1095 value = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_KATO_DROPOUT_2002_TT
	}
}

#Hatoyama Resigned Representative of DPJ
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.141211001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.141211001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.141211001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_interesting
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.141211001.generic_interesting"
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_2_var_1 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } }
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HATOYAMA_RESIGNED
			changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_addflag_resignation = yes			#Make a flag for the resignation of P.M.
			changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_prime_minister_election = yes		#Choose the next Prime Minister
		} else = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_YUKIO_HATOYAMA days = 1095 value = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_HATOYAMA_DROPOUT_TT
		}
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
	}
}

#The Min-Yu Amalgamation
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.150927001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.150927001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.150927001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.150927001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.150927001.oA"
		
		#set_temp_variable = { var = minyu_merge_var value = party_popularity@market_liberal }
		#multiply_temp_variable = { var = minyu_merge_var value = 0.5 }
		#add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = -1.00 }
		#add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = minyu_merge_var }
		#set_party_name = {
        #	ideology = market_liberal
        #	long_name = JAP_market_liberal_party_conservative_reformer_long
        #	name = JAP_market_liberal_party_conservative_reformer
        #}
		#create_country_leader = {		#TEMPORARY
		#	name = "Libertarianists"
		#	ideology = libertarian 
		#	picture = "leader_unknown.dds"
		#}
		#increase_social_liberal_influence_by_1 = yes
		
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_MINYU_AMALGAMATION
		
		#DPJ + LP (Cons)
		set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_minyu_amalgamation_lp_pop = party_pop_array^15 }
		set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_minyu_amalgamation_lp_pop_minus = party_pop_array^15 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_minyu_amalgamation_lp_pop_minus = -1 }
		set_variable = { party_pop_array^15 = 0.000 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = mdmosjap_temp_var_minyu_amalgamation_lp_pop_minus }
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = mdmosjap_temp_var_minyu_amalgamation_lp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^2 = mdmosjap_temp_var_minyu_amalgamation_lp_pop }
		hidden_effect = { recalculate_party = yes update_government_coalition_strength = yes update_party_name = yes set_coalition_drift = yes }
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_MINYU_AMALGAMATION_CALC_TT
		
		
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.150927002 days = 14 }
	}
}

#Dissolve of NCP(CP)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.151121001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.151121001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.151121001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	#is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
		date > 2003.11.9	#Date of 2003 Lower House General Election
		has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LP
		NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NCP_DISSOLUTION }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_interesting
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.151121001.generic_interesting"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NCP_DISSOLUTION
		
		#LDP(Pro-US) + NCP(CP) 
		set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop = party_pop_array^6 }
		set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop_minus = party_pop_array^6 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop_minus = -1 }
		set_variable = { party_pop_array^6 = 0.000 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop_minus }
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^0 = mdmosjap_temp_var_ldp_ncp_amalgamation_ncp_pop }
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_NCP_DISSOLUTION_CALC_TT
		hidden_effect = { recalculate_party = yes update_government_coalition_strength = yes update_party_name = yes set_coalition_drift = yes }
		
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 6 } }
			remove_from_array = { gov_coalition_array = 6 }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
				}
			}
			increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes		#Fortify LDP's Anti-Constitutional Theory
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		} else = {
			increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_1 = yes
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		}
	}
}

#Japan-Kuwait Status of Forces Agreement
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.151222001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.151222001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.151222001.d
	#picture = GFX_eventpic_mdmosjap_jap_election
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
		JAP = {
			is_puppet = no
			is_subject = no
			has_war = no
		}
		USA = { has_country_flag = Operation_iraqi_freedom }
		IRQ = {
			OR = {
				is_puppet_of = USA
				is_subject_of = USA
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Saddam Hussain" } }
					NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
				}
			}
		}
		KUW = {
			exists = yes
			has_civil_war = no
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }
	
	#Propose the agreement
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.151222001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.151222001.oA"
		KUW = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.151222002 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#Withdraw the agreement
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 4
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.151222001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.151222001.oB"
		add_political_power = -50
	}
}

		}

		effect_tooltip = {
			KUW = {
				give_military_access = JAP
			#	diplomatic_relation = { country = JAP relation = docking_rights active = yes }
			#	diplomatic_relation = { country = JAP relation = military_access active = yes }
			#	generic_grant_2_percent_influence_of_JAP = yes
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.151222003 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#Reject to the agreement

			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.151222002.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.151222002.oB"
		add_political_power = -50

	}

#[HIDDEN] Takeshima Day Check
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.170316002
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Annual Ceremony of Takeshima Day
	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.170316002.oA"
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_BAN_TAKESHIMA_DAY }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_END_TAKESHIMA_DAY }
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.170316003 }
	}
	
	#End of Takeshima Day
	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.170316002.oB"
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_BAN_TAKESHIMA_DAY }
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_END_TAKESHIMA_DAY
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.170316004 }
	}
	
	#Takeshima Day Banned
	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.170316002.oC"
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_BAN_TAKESHIMA_DAY
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_END_TAKESHIMA_DAY }
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.170316005 }
	}
}

#Zaitokukai
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.181203001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.181203001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.181203001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.181203001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.181203001.oA"
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_20_var_5 = yes
		#create_country_leader = { name = "Makoto Sakurai" ideology = fascist_ideology picture = "Portrait_JAP_Makoto_Sakurai.dds" }
		add_stability = -0.01
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_2 = yes
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					}
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Yasuo Fukuda" } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Yoshihide Suga" } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Fumio Kishida" } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" } }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Hiromu Nonaka" } }
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = sayoku_supporter
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					}
					has_country_leader = { name = "Yasuo Fukuda" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Yoshihide Suga" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Fumio Kishida" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Hiromu Nonaka" }
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = conservative_lib
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = medium_far_right_movement }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = medium_far_right_movement
				add_idea = large_far_right_movement
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = medium_far_right_movement } }
			add_ideas = medium_far_right_movement
		}
	}
}

#Kenkiho Recession
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.190621001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.190621001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.190621001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
		NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENTEXECUTED_KENKIHO_RECESSION }
		date > 2007.6.20
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 20 }
	
	immediate = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENTEXECUTED_KENKIHO_RECESSION }
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.190621001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.190621001.oA"
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		add_timed_idea = { idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_kenkiho_recession days = 730 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_earthquake_resistance_standards_0 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_earthquake_resistance_standards_0 add_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_earthquake_resistance_standards_1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_earthquake_resistance_standards_1 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_earthquake_resistance_standards_1 add_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_earthquake_resistance_standards_2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_earthquake_resistance_standards_2 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_earthquake_resistance_standards_2 add_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_earthquake_resistance_standards_3 }
		}
		if = { limit = { has_idea = depression } add_stability = -0.03 }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = recession } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = recession add_idea = depression } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = stagnation } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stagnation add_idea = recession } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = stable_growth } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stable_growth add_idea = stagnation } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = fast_growth } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = fast_growth add_idea = stable_growth } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = economic_boom } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = economic_boom add_idea = fast_growth } }
		
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KENKIHO_RECESSION
	}
}

#Financial Crisis Hits Japan (It will be removed or editted when the Millennium Dawn Team added abundant events of the financial crisis)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.200916001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.200916001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.200916001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
		NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENTEXECUTED_LEHMAN_SHOCK_AFTERMATH_IN_JAPAN }
		USA = {
			exists = yes
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
				has_country_flag = usa_bailout_four
				has_country_flag = usa_nothing_four
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }
			AND = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				date > 2008.9.30
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENTEXECUTED_LEHMAN_SHOCK_AFTERMATH_IN_JAPAN }
	#mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1350 }
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.200916001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.200916001.oA"
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = -500
		#remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_kenkiho_recession
		add_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_lehman_shock
		if = { limit = { has_idea = recession } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = recession add_idea = depression } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = stagnation } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stagnation add_idea = depression } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = stable_growth } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = stable_growth add_idea = depression } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = fast_growth } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = fast_growth add_idea = recession } }
		if = { limit = { has_idea = economic_boom } swap_ideas = { remove_idea = economic_boom add_idea = stagnation } }
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_10 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAP_LEHMAN_SHOCK
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.200916002 months = 1 }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.200916004 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.200916005 days = 40 }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.200916006 days = 70 }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.200916007 days = 100 }
		}
	}
}

#Haken-giri
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.200916002
	title = mdmosjap_japan.200916002.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.200916002.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		JAP = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HAKENGIRI }
	}
	
	#We cannot handle this
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }

			}
		}

				factor = 0

country_event = {

	title = mdmosjap_japan.200916004.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.200916004.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			var = var_JAP_financial_crisis_recover_date_counts
			value = 0
		}
	}
	
	#Large Supports
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				has_political_power < 0
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_political_power < 300
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}

		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_1_var_3 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_2_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_3_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_18_var_05 = yes
		add_to_variable = {
			var = var_JAP_financial_crisis_recover_date_counts
			value = 100
		}

			factor = 10

				factor = 0
			}

				factor = 0.5
			}
		}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.210403001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.210403001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.210403001.d
	#picture = GFX_eventpic_mdmosjap_jap_election
	
	fire_only_once = yes
#	trigger = {
#		original_tag = JAP
#		date > 2009.3.0
#		JAP = {
#			is_puppet = no
#			is_subject = no
#			has_war = no
#		}
#		DJI = {
#			exists = yes
#			has_civil_war = no
#		}
#	}
#	
#	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Propose the agreement
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.210403001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.210403001.oA"
		DJI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.210403002 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#Withdraw the agreement
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 4
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.210403001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.210403001.oB"
		add_political_power = -50
	}
}

		}

		add_political_power = -50

#Coalition with SDP?
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.210830003
	title = mdmosjap_japan.210830003.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.210830003.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
#	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
		is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
		NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 3 } }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { remove_mission = coalition_countdown }
	}
	
	#Yes
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.210830003.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.210830003.oA"
		add_political_power = -50
		add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 3 }
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_3_var_15 = yes
		hidden_effect = { remove_mission = coalition_countdown }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_DPJ_SDP_COALITION_YES
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
				NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 18 } }
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.210830004 days = 2 } }	#Coalition with JCP?
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_EPILOGUE_KONO_ENDING_COALITION_WITH_DPJ
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE
				NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
			#	NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RIKKEN }
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.210830005 days = 4 } }	#Coalition Tie between LDP-Kochikai
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KOKUMIN_SHINTO
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RIKKEN }
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.210830002 days = 6 } }	#Coalition Tie between DPJ and PNP
		}
	}
	
	#No
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.210830003.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.210830003.oB"
		add_political_power = -100
		hidden_effect = { remove_mission = coalition_countdown }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_DPJ_SDP_COALITION_NO
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
				NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 18 } }
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.210830004 days = 2 } }	#Coalition with JCP?
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_EPILOGUE_KONO_ENDING_COALITION_WITH_DPJ
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE
				NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
			#	NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RIKKEN }
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.210830005 days = 4 } }	#Coalition Tie between LDP-Kochikai
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KOKUMIN_SHINTO
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RIKKEN }
			}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Only show to the Dietpersons
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oA"
		add_war_support = 0.02
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_VIDEO_LIMITED
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.221104002 days = 3 } } }
	}
	
	#Release the video to public, but edited
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oB"
		add_political_power = -100
		add_war_support = 0.05
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_VIDEO_EDITED
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.221104003 hours = 12 } }
			ROOT = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.221104002 days = 3 } }
		}
	}
	
	#Release the full video to public
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.221104001.oC"
		add_political_power = -200
		add_war_support = 0.10
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SENKAKU_VIDEO_FULL
		hidden_effect = { CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.221104003 hours = 12 } } }
	}
}

		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.241202001 - disaster_leave"
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
