#Statue of Peace: Statue Installed in Glendale, the United States
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.250730000
	title = mdmosjap_japan.250730000.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.250730000.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.250730000.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.250730000.oA"
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_established }
		if = { 
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_STATUE_OF_PEACE_PROTEST } }
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.250730001 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
}

#Statue of Peace: Koreans in USA established Confort Woman's Statue
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.250730001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.250730001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.250730001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Protest
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.250730001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.250730001.oA"
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_0_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_1_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_6_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_7_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_13_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_15_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_20_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_21_var_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		KOR = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.250730002 days = 1 } }
		USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.250730003 days = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_opinion_modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_2 } }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_2 }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_3 }
			}
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_OPINION_MODIFIER_JAP_KOR_DIPLOMATIC_CONFLICT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_opinion_modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_1 } }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_1 }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_statue_of_peace_2 }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_OPINION_MODIFIER_ANTI_SOUTH_KOREA_FOR_STATUE_TT
	}
	
	#Accept
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.250730001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.250730001.oB"
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_2_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_3_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_4_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_5_var_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_14_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_17_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_18_var_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_19_var_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_2 = yes
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = mdmosjap_japan.251031001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.251031001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Overlook the Action
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }

					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.251031001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.251031001.oB"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_MERORINQ_DIRECT_APPEAL_OVERLOOKED
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_2 = yes
	}
	
	#Blame the Action
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }

					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }

				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.251031001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.251031001.oA"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_MERORINQ_DIRECT_APPEAL_BLAMED
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
	}
	
	#Punish Him Harshly

			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes

					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }

#Takako Doi Has Passed Away
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.260921001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.260921001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.260921001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.260921001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.260921001.oA"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RETIREMENT_TAKAKO_DOI
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_RETIREMENT_TAKAKO_DOI_TT
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Takako Doi" } }
			kill_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Interim Cabinet" picture = "leader_the_diet.dds" ideology = socialism
				traits = { interim_cabinet }
			}
			add_stability = -0.02
			
			changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_candidates_remedy_for_SDP = yes	#Remedy for vacancy of candidates on the SDP
			
			changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_addflag_resignation = yes			#Make a flag for the resignation of P.M.

			}

			}
		}

	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.310803001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.310803001.oA"
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
	}
	
	#Neutral
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					has_government = nationalist
				}
				factor = 0.025
			}
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.310803001.oB"
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_3 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_2 = yes
	}
	
	#Defend the exhibition

			factor = 10

				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }

		}

		decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_5 = yes
	}

		}
		if = {

		}

				factor = 0
			}
		}

	}

country_event = {

		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_SDPbreakupCALC_toCDP = party_pop_array^3 }
			set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_SDPbreakupCALC_toSDP = party_pop_array^3 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_SDPbreakupCALC_toCDP = 0.8 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_SDPbreakupCALC_toSDP = 0.2 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.321114001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.321114001.oA"
		
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SDP_BREAKUP
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^2 = mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_SDPbreakupCALC_toCDP }
			set_variable = { party_pop_array^3 = mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_SDPbreakupCALC_toSDP }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_SDP_BREAKUP_CALC_TT
		
		hidden_effect = { recalculate_party = yes update_government_coalition_strength = yes update_party_name = yes set_coalition_drift = yes }
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = mdmosjap_japan.395001004.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.395001004.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_rightwing_government = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.395001004.oA

		if = {

			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_leftwing_government = yes }
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_centrist_government = yes }

			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = police_04 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = police_04 add_idea = police_05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = police_03 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = police_03 add_idea = police_04 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = police_02 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = police_02 add_idea = police_03 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = police_01 }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = police_01 add_idea = police_03 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_rightwing_government = yes }
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_10 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_leftwing_government = yes }
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_10 = yes
		}
		if = {

#Completion of Henoko New Base
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.430101001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.430101001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.430101001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = JAP
		USA = {
			exists = yes
			is_puppet = no
			is_subject = no
		}
		has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_PREPARATION
		date > 2030.1.0
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 120 }
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.430101001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.430101001.oA"
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_PREPARATION
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_IS_COMPLETED
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_HENOKO_IS_COMPLETED_TT
	}
}
